# <a name="microsoft-365-encryption-chains"></a><span data-ttu-id="8190a-103">Microsoft 365 加密链</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8190a-103">Microsoft 365 encryption chains</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8190a-104">Microsoft 365 利用许多不同的证书提供程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8190a-104">Microsoft 365 leverages a number of different certificate providers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8190a-105">下面介绍了客户在访问 Microsoft 365 时可能遇到的已知 Microsoft 365 根证书的完整列表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8190a-105">The following describes the complete list of known Microsoft 365 root certificates that customers may encounter when accessing Microsoft 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8190a-106">有关可能需要在您自己的基础结构中安装的证书的信息，请参阅"为 Microsoft [365](https://docs.microsoft.com/microsoft-365/enterprise/plan-for-third-party-ssl-certificates)规划第三方 SSL 证书"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8190a-106">For information on the certificates you may need to install in your own infrastructure, see [Plan for third-party SSL certificates for Microsoft 365](https://docs.microsoft.com/microsoft-365/enterprise/plan-for-third-party-ssl-certificates).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8190a-107">以下证书信息适用于 Microsoft 365 的所有全球和国家云实例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8190a-107">The following certificate information applies to all worldwide and national cloud instances of Microsoft 365.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8190a-108">Last updated： **10/16/2020**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8190a-108">Last updated: **10/16/2020**</span></span>
